<div class="para">解放以来<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />广东发现的新石器时代遗址或遗物地点<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />约有四<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=327226498813097597389946285" />五百处<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />经试掘和发掘的约四<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=327226498813097597389946285" />五十处<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=950481408382793485046963025" />清理墓葬二百多座<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />获得各种文化遗物数以万计<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />为探索广东原始社会的历史<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />提供了珍贵的实物资料<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=950481408382793485046963025" />在各地发现的文化遗存中<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />已经提出了两个文化名称<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />即西樵山文化和石峡文化<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=950481408382793485046963025" /></div>
<div class="para">石峡文化是1977年提出的④<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=950481408382793485046963025" />它以曲江县石峡遗址下层和墓葬代表<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=327226498813097597389946285" />壶组合<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" <div class="para">西樵山遗址发现于1958年<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />西樵山文化是1960年提出的<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />而且对探索与华南<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=327226498813097597389946285" />东南沿海地区有关原始文化的关系<img class="pchar" <div class="para">西樵山遗址位于广东南海县官山镇西樵山<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />它原是一座古火山丘<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />周边长约13公里<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />直径约4公里<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=950481408382793485046963025" />山峰高度一般为100-200米<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />最高峰大科峰为300余米<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=950481408382793485046963025" />山体主要由粗面岩<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=327226498813097597389946285" />火山碎屑岩和石英岩构成<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=950481408382793485046963025" />在东北部的火石迳等有燧石<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=327226498813097597389946285" />玛瑙出露<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=699628396194950359649413178" />在西部的马鞍山及山顶的锦岩等洞穴有霏细岩岩脉<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=950481408382793485046963025" />西樵山山麓周围分布着新老两套洪积冲积扇<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />山下连接开阔的珠江三角洲冲积平原<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=950481408382793485046963025" />从新石器以至更早的时候起<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />便有人类在山上及周围一带采石制器<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />劳动生息<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=950481408382793485046963025" /><sup>[3]</sup><a class="anchor-inline" name="ref_[3]_865930">&nbsp;</a></div>

<div class="para">由此可见<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />西樵山遗址是一处大型的<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=327226498813097597389946285" />延续年代很长的<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=327226498813097597389946285" />供应范围很广的石器制作场<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />这是最突出和最主要的<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=950481408382793485046963025" />同时也有生产生活的遗址<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />这也是不可否认的<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=950481408382793485046963025" />总之<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />西樵山遗址中包涵了新石器各个阶段的遗存<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />主要是中<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=327226498813097597389946285" />晚期遗存<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=950481408382793485046963025" /><sup>[3]</sup><a class="anchor-inline" name="ref_[3]_865930">&nbsp;</a></div>

class="anchor-2"></a><a name="sub865930_6_4" class="anchor-2"></a><a name="遗址文化_文化内涵" class="anchor-2"></a><span class="headline-content">文化内涵</span></h3><div class="para">西樵山文化因1958年首先发现于南海县西樵山而得名<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=950481408382793485046963025" />在一段时间内<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />它是专指西樵山遗址本身的遗存<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=950481408382793485046963025" />从发现的材料看<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />西樵山文化应当是分布于珠江三角洲地区的一种新石器时代的原始文化<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=950481408382793485046963025" />它区别于封开黄岩洞类型和英德青塘类型的洞穴遗址<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />区别于韩江流域陈桥村类型的贝丘遗址<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />也不同于粤北的石峡文化<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />具有其自身的特点<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=950481408382793485046963025" /></div><h3 class="headline-2"><a name="6_5" class="anchor-2"></a><a name="sub865930_6_5" class="headline-content">文化早期</span></h3><div class="para">早期以西樵山火石迳等细石器遗存为代表<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />其上限年代暂推定为距今七<img
